event = {
	id = 2003007
	random = no
	country = GER

	name = "反共产国际协约 "
	desc = "共产国际日益扩张的影响是很多国家领导人担忧的对象。１９３ ７年，德国与意大利和日本达成了为期五年的协议，彼此共享情 报，并互相协助以对抗共产主义的影响。 "
  	style = 2
	picture = "anti_comitern_pact"
	decision_picture = "decision_anticominternpact"

	decision = {
		exists = JAP
		exists = ITA
		exists = SOV
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = ITA }
			war = { country = GER country = JAP }
			war = { country = JAP country = ITA }
			alliance = { country = GER country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = ITA country = SOV }
		}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { war = { country = ITA country = ETH } }
			war = { country = SPA country = SPR } 
			year = 1937
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { war = { country = ITA country = ETH } }
			AND = { war = { country = SPA country = SPR } random = 50 } 
			year = 1937
		}
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = ITA }
			war = { country = GER country = JAP }
			war = { country = JAP country = ITA }
			alliance = { country = GER country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = ITA country = SOV }
		}
	}

	date = { day = 20 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 1 month = december year = 1938 }

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 95
		name = "与意大利和日本谈判协约 "
		command = { type = domestic which = freedom value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 1 }
		command = { type = relation which = SOV value = -20 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 72 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 73 }
	}
	action_b = {
		ai_chance = 5
		name = EVT_71_ACTD
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = -1 }
	}
}

	id = 40042
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = { year = 1936 exists = AUS }
	
	decision_trigger = {
		atwar = no
		NOT = {
            alliance = { country = GER country = AUS }
			war = { country = AUS country = GER }
            puppet = { country = aus country = ger }
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
                atwar = no
		exists = AUS
		exists = GER
		NOT = {
            alliance = { country = GER country = AUS }
			war = { country = AUS country = GER }
            puppet = { country = aus country = ger }
		}
	}

	name = "德奥协定 "
	desc = "１９３６年７月１１日，德国和奥地利官员在讨价还价后达成了 一项协议。其中最重要的是德国将保证奥地利的主权。协议中还 包括了一项秘密条款：奥地利纳粹党将会得到特赦并恢复政治活 动，撤除对纳粹言论的审查，在内阁中任命亲纳粹的人士。 "
	style = 2
	picture = "ger_40042_austro_schuschnigg"

	date = { day = 9 month = july year = 1936 }
	offset = 7
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = august year = 1936 }

	action_a = {
		name = "这将是德奥合并的第一步，也是必须的一步 "
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = trigger which = 40414 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "没必要隐藏我们的真实意图 "
		ai_chance = 1
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
		command = { type = belligerence which = GER value = 10 }
	}
}

		}												# BHT1.5
		OR = {											# BHT1.5
			ai = GER									# BHT1.5
			NOT = { flag = normal	}						# BHT1.5
		}												# BHT1.5
	}

	name = "EVT_2605_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_2605_DESC"
	style = 2
	picture = "Mol_Rib"

	date = { day = 24 month = august year = 1939 }
	offset = 60
	deathdate = { day = 28 month = december year = 1941 }



	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME2605A" # We shall never forget this!
		ai_chance = 90
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = relation which = GER value = -30 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = Pact_Broken }
	}

		name = "ACTIONNAME2605B" # This means war!
		ai_chance = 10
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = war which = GER }
		command = { type = clrflag which = Pact_Broken }
	}
}

#  Germany Invades Poland without our Blessing! (Edited by 兰々)
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 2650
	random = no
	country = SOV

	name = "德国未经我们许可就入侵了波兰！"
	desc = "EVT_2650_DESC"
	style = 2

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 20
	deathdate = { day = 28 month = january year = 1940 }

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			event = 2013 # Historical Pact
			event = 2015 # Unholy Alliance, rejected or signed
			event = 2016 # Limited Pact
		}
		OR = {
			non_aggression = { country = GER country = SOV }
			guarantee = { country = SOV country = POL }
		}
		atwar = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				under_attack = POL
				war = { country = GER country = POL }
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = POL }
					AND = {												# BHT1.5
						exists = POL									# BHT1.5
						OR = {											# BHT1.5
							alliance = { country = POL country = GER }	# BHT1.5
							puppet = { country = POL country = GER }	# BHT1.5
						}												# BHT1.5
					}													# BHT1.5
				}
				OR = {													# BHT1.5
					NOT = { exists = U00 }								# BHT1.5
					AND = {												# BHT1.5
						exists = U00									# BHT1.5
						OR = {											# BHT1.5
							alliance = { country = U00 country = GER }	# BHT1.5
							puppet = { country = U00 country = GER }	# BHT1.5
						}												# BHT1.5
					}													# BHT1.5
				}														# BHT1.5
				OR = {
					control = { province = 485 data = GER } # Warsaw
					control = { province = 485 data = POL }				# BHT1.5
					control = { province = 485 data = U00 }				# BHT1.5
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			ai = GER													# BHT1.5
			NOT = { flag = normal }										# BHT1.5
		}
	}

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_2650_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 90
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = relation which = GER value = -50 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "EVT_2650_ACTB"
		ai_chance = 10
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = POL value = 50 }
		command = { type = war which = GER }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 2668
	random = no
	country = SOV

	name = "德国未经我们许可就入侵了波兰！ "
	desc = "EVT_2650_DESC"
	style = 2

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 20
	deathdate = { day = 28 month = january year = 1940 }

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			event = 2013 # Historical Pact
			event = 2015 # Unholy Alliance, rejected or signed
			event = 2016 # Limited Pact
		}
		OR = {
			non_aggression = { country = GER country = SOV }
			guarantee = { country = SOV country = POL }
		}
		atwar = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				under_attack = POL
				war = { country = GER country = POL }
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = POL }
					AND = {
						exists = POL
						OR = {
							alliance = { country = POL country = GER }
							puppet = { country = POL country = GER }
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = U00 }
					AND = {
						exists = U00
						OR = {
							alliance = { country = U00 country = GER }
							puppet = { country = U00 country = GER }
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					control = { province = 485 data = GER } # Warsaw
					control = { province = 485 data = POL }
					control = { province = 485 data = U00 }
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { ai = GER }
		flag = normal
	}

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_2650_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 20
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = relation which = GER value = -50 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "EVT_2650_ACTB"
		ai_chance = 80
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = POL value = 50 }
		command = { type = war which = GER }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 40013
	country = GER
	random = no

	trigger = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }

	name = "德国空军征召民航飞行员 "
	desc = "汉莎航空，此时最成功的欧洲航空公司，为德国空军提供了大量 高素质的人员，囊括了从低级管理人员、后勤人员到飞行员和高 级空军将领各个层次。 "
	style = 2
	picture = "40013_Luftwaffe_recall_comercial_pilots"

	date = { day = 6 month = september year = 1939 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1940 }

	action_a = {
		name = "征召俯冲和截击中队 "
		ai_chance = 45
		command = { type = dissent value = 2 }
		command = { type = resource which = money value = -100 }
		command = { type = add_division value = cas when = 0 }
		command = { type = add_division value = interceptor when = 2 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "征召轰炸和俯冲中队 "
		ai_chance = 45
		command = { type = dissent value = 2 }
		command = { type = resource which = money value = -100 }
		command = { type = add_division value = cas when = 0 }
		command = { type = add_division value = tactical_bomber when = 2 where =  escort }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "用于商业航空服务 "
		ai_chance = 10
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
		command = { type = resource which = money value = 100 }
	}	
}
